        const player = componentEvent.player;
        system.run(() => openTownshipBlockUiFromBlock(block, player));
      }
    });

    registry.registerCustomComponent("township:build_recorder_component", {
      onPlayerInteract(componentEvent) {
        const block = componentEvent.block;
        const player = componentEvent.player;
        system.run(() => openTownshipBlockUiFromBlock(block, player));
      }
    });

    registry.registerCustomComponent("township:ground_leveler_component", {
      onPlayerInteract(componentEvent) {
        const block = componentEvent.block;
        const player = componentEvent.player;
        system.run(() => openTownshipBlockUiFromBlock(block, player));
      }
    });
  } catch (error) {
    sendDebugLogError(ADDON_NAME, "Register Township Block Components", error);
  }
}

try {
  system.beforeEvents.startup.subscribe((event) => {
    registerTownshipBlockComponents(event);
  });
} catch (error) {
  sendDebugLogError(ADDON_NAME, "Subscribe startup block components", error);
}


// v1.0.59: custom block components removed from block JSON because they caused non-road blocks to disappear on the user's current Bedrock build.
// UI access is restored through crouch-near-block and itemUseOn fallback.

// v1.0.59 stable fallback: when holding an item, tap/use it on a Township UI block to open its menu.
try {
  world.afterEvents.itemUseOn.subscribe((event) => {
    try {
      const block = event.block;
      const player = event.source;
      if (!block || !player) return;
      if (block.typeId === FOUNDING_STONE_ID || isLotMarkerType(block.typeId) || isBuildLotRecorderType(block.typeId) || block.typeId === GROUND_LEVELER_ID || block.typeId === BUILD_RECORDER_ID) {
        system.run(() => openTownshipBlockUiFromBlock(block, player));
      }
    } catch (error) {
      sendDebugLogError(ADDON_NAME, "ItemUseOn UI Fallback", error);
    }
  });
} catch (error) {
  sendDebugLogError(ADDON_NAME, "Subscribe itemUseOn UI Fallback", error);
}

// Primary stable path: global player-place event.
try {
  world.afterEvents.playerPlaceBlock.subscribe((event) => {
    try {
      const block = event.block;
      if (block && block.typeId === FOUNDING_STONE_ID) registerTownFromBlock(block, event.player);
      else if (block && isBuildLotRecorderType(block.typeId)) registerBuildLotFromBlock(block, event.player);
      else if (block && isLotMarkerType(block.typeId)) registerLotMarkerFromBlock(block, event.player);
      else if (block && block.typeId === GROUND_LEVELER_ID) registerGroundLevelerFromBlock(block, event.player);
      else if (block && block.typeId === BUILD_RECORDER_ID) registerBuildRecorderFromBlock(block, event.player);
    } catch (error) {
      sendDebugLogError(ADDON_NAME, "Global Place Event", error);
    }
  });
} catch (error) {
  sendDebugLogError(ADDON_NAME, "Subscribe playerPlaceBlock", error);
}

try {
  world.afterEvents.playerBreakBlock.subscribe((event) => {
    try {
      const typeId = event.brokenBlockPermutation?.type?.id ?? event.brokenBlockPermutation?.typeId;
      if (typeId === FOUNDING_STONE_ID) cleanupTownAt(event.block.location, event.dimension.id, event.player);
      else if (isLotMarkerType(typeId)) cleanupLotAt(event.block.location, event.dimension.id, event.player);
      else if (typeId === BUILD_RECORDER_ID) {
        messagePlayer(event.player, "§eTownship Build Recorder removed.");
      }
      else if (typeId === GROUND_LEVELER_ID) {
        for (const town of getTowns()) {
          if (!town || town.dimensionId !== event.dimension.id) continue;
          town.jobs = getJobs(town).filter(job => !(job.type === "ground_leveler" && job.location && job.location.x === event.block.location.x && job.location.y === event.block.location.y && job.location.z === event.block.location.z));
        }
        saveTowns(getTowns());
        messagePlayer(event.player, "§eTownship Ground Leveler job removed.");
      }
    } catch (error) {
      sendDebugLogError(ADDON_NAME, "Global Break Event", error);
    }
  });
} catch (error) {
  sendDebugLogError(ADDON_NAME, "Subscribe playerBreakBlock", error);
}

try {
  world.afterEvents.playerSpawn.subscribe((event) => {
    try {
      const player = event.player;
      if (!player || scriptLoadedAnnounced.has(player.id)) return;
      scriptLoadedAnnounced.add(player.id);
      system.runTimeout(() => {
        messagePlayer(player, `§7Township script loaded v${VERSION}.`);
      }, 5);
    } catch (error) {
      sendDebugLogError(ADDON_NAME, "Player Spawn Message", error);
    }
  });
} catch (error) {
  sendDebugLogError(ADDON_NAME, "Subscribe playerSpawn", error);
}

system.runTimeout(() => {
  loadTowns();
  sendSystemMessage(`§7Township script initialized v${VERSION}.`);
}, 1);

system.runInterval(() => {
  tickCounter += 5;
  processTowns();
  processLotBorderPreview();
  processSneakStatusChecks();
}, 5);
=== SOURCE FILE END ===

--- CONTENT ---
Township Changelog
Version: v1.0.25

Stable base before this build:
- v1.0.24 had working Founding Stone, Lot Marker, Ground Leveler, road preview/particles, bigger township area, and five automatic building variants.

Critical update workflow change:
- This build stops using fresh UUIDs for every export.
- From v1.0.25 forward, Township should update as the same add-on by keeping the same pack/module UUIDs and increasing only the manifest/module/dependency versions.
- This is required for better mobile update behavior and for preserving world dynamic-property data tied to the behavior pack identity.

Fixed Township pack identity going forward:
- BP header UUID: efb55785-5680-46d8-b4c7-8f8a2cddf364
- BP data module UUID: 7e320f0f-f615-4230-8b83-e6a0ffdc87cd
- BP script module UUID: 0546c591-16c9-4f60-bc44-fec4a749892c
- RP header UUID: 6effc74f-a22d-46d5-95f2-778c00fdfb9b
- RP resources module UUID: 7d1e0f0c-e786-41df-870d-72e9ea96ed10
- Namespace: township
- Current version: 1.0.25

Required future update rules:
- Keep BP header UUID the same.
- Keep BP module UUIDs the same.
- Keep RP header UUID the same.
- Keep RP module UUID the same.
- Increase BP header.version.
- Increase every BP module.version.
- Increase RP header.version.
- Increase every RP module.version.
- Update BP dependency on the RP to the new RP version.
- Update RP dependency on the BP to the new BP version.
- Keep RP header.pack_scope = "world".
- Do not use fresh UUIDs unless intentionally creating a separate add-on.

Gameplay and bug fixes:
- Replaced the earlier "same building in different styles" system with five more distinct building shapes that share one Township starter style family.
- New automatic building variants:
  1. Small Cottage
  2. Narrow House
  3. Wide House
  4. Workshop
  5. Storage Cottage
- These buildings use different footprints/silhouettes instead of only swapping materials.
- Kept the same starter style family: oak logs/planks, spruce roofs, simple chimneys, practical interiors.
- Reworked interior placement so beds, chests, furnaces, crafting tables, and barrels sit against interior walls instead of cluttering the center or embedding into the back wall.
- Changed door block ID from minecraft:oak_door to minecraft:wooden_door for Bedrock compatibility.
- Changed bed block ID from minecraft:red_bed to minecraft:bed for Bedrock compatibility.
- Kept directional door and bed state placement logic.
- Improved road avoidance by expanding blocked lot bounds for road pathfinding and road brush placement.
- Removed the short broken-road-stub fallback when no safe road route is found.
- Roads should now either find a safer path around lots or fail without creating a short partial road.

Known items to test:
- Confirm this imports as an update over v1.0.24 instead of a new separate add-on.
- Confirm existing township data persists when updating from v1.0.24 to v1.0.25.
- Confirm new buildings look meaningfully different, not just material swaps.
- Confirm real doors and beds appear correctly.
- Confirm furniture is against the walls.
- Confirm roads avoid other lots better and do not create short broken stubs.

Known limitations:
- Door/bed orientation still needs testing in all four Lot Marker facing directions.
- Road routing is still prototype-level; it avoids registered lots but does not yet build a formal township road grid.
- The builder still uses a vanilla villager base and may wander outside active construction.

- House door placement now follows that offset path where possible.

- Road start point now uses the offset side entrance rather than the center marker line.
- Ground Leveler top fill now uses dirt instead of coarse dirt.

- Placing a Township Founding Stone now queues a township area preparation job.
- The township prep job clears and levels a large starting work area around the Founding Stone.
- The top fill layer is dirt, not coarse dirt.
- The township prep job marks the usable build boundary with oak fence and periodic torches so the player can see the current township limit.
- The full 192-block claim is still reserved, but the initial prep work focuses on a practical large starting work area to avoid destroying an extreme area all at once.

- Check if houses now sit on filled ground instead of over dips.
- Check whether side fencing remains after houses build.
- Check whether the offset path feels better with the Lot Marker still centered.
- Check whether the township boundary fence/torch marker is useful or too heavy visually.

- Farm patches include farmland, wheat, water, and a composter as the temporary farmer job block.

- During initial township setup, the script attempts to add a temporary ticking area for the active quadrant.
- When that quadrant finishes, it removes the temporary ticking area and moves to the next quadrant.

- This uses Bedrock command-based ticking areas from script and must be tested in-game on Android.

Purpose:
- Test whether quadrant loading lets the initial clear/level/boundary finish more reliably.
- Prevent the township prep from becoming one huge hanging job.
- Keep the main/starter lot from starting until quadrant setup completes.

Still not changed:
- Active lot/build/road ticking areas are not implemented yet.
- Building presets are not reworked in this build.
- Township size/radius is not changed in this build.

--- CONTENT ---
Township Add-On Change Log

Project Name: Township
Namespace: township

Design Direction
- The add-on is now named Township.
- The main founding block is named Township Founding Stone.
- All player-facing Township blocks should start with "Township" for easier creative-menu searching.
- Townships use a reserved territory system: a full claim is reserved immediately, while usable build radius can grow later by tier.
- Townships cannot overlap. Current planned full claim radius is 96 blocks, meaning new Township Founding Stones should be rejected if another active township center is within 192 blocks.
- Central block is not called Township Core in-game. Use Township Founding Stone.

Long-Term Systems Planned
- Township Founding Stone creates and manages a township.
- Township Builder arrives after a delay if the town has no builder.
- Builders visually construct buildings block-by-block while scripts place blocks.
- Township lots/parcels will use Township Signposts.
- Lot sizes are planned as Small 11x11, Medium 15x15, Large 21x21, and Special for central/plaza/wall/gate structures.
- Roads will use special Township Road blocks and can upgrade.
- Auto Roads controls creation of new roads.
- Auto Upgrade controls upgrading existing buildings and roads.
- Roads bordering a lot should upgrade to match the highest nearby lot level when Auto Upgrade is on.
- Township storage is hidden script data, not directly visible to the player.
- Township Donation Crate is the planned player-facing intake for town supplies.
- Storage buildings are visual/villager access points, not the player-visible town inventory.
- Villager wealth should be tied to individual assigned villagers.
- If a villager dies, their personal money/reputation resets or is lost, while the building remains.
- Villager equipment/tool upgrades should be limited by assigned lot level.
- Builders are not directly limited by a raw number; builder capacity is controlled by Builder House-type buildings.

v1.0.1
- First prototype package created.
- Added Behavior Pack and Resource Pack.
- Added pack icons.
- Added Township Founding Stone concept.
- Added scripted township registration logic.
- Added no-overlap township rule.
- Added delayed builder arrival concept.
- Builder is a persistent vanilla villager named Township Builder for the first test.
- Added Debug Log Reader bridge hook using scriptevent debuglog:error.

Known issues found in v1.0.1
- Township Founding Stone did not appear in creative search.
- Behavior Pack and Resource Pack did not activate together automatically.
- BP/RP dependency linking was incomplete.
- Block custom component attachment needed correction.

v1.0.2
- Fixed BP/RP linking by adding reverse dependency.
- Corrected custom block component attachment to use minecraft:custom_components.
- Added creative item catalog entry so the block should appear in creative search under Township / Founding.
- Kept the same first-test goal: place Township Founding Stone, create township, prevent overlap, spawn Township Builder after delay.

Current test target
- Import Township_v1_0_2.mcaddon.
- Activate the pack and verify BP/RP link together.
- Search creative inventory for Township or Founding.
- Place Township Founding Stone.
- Confirm it creates a township.
- Wait for Township Builder arrival.
- Try placing a second Township Founding Stone within 192 blocks and confirm it is rejected.

Next planned version
v1.0.3
- Fix any remaining import, creative visibility, dependency, or content-log errors from v1.0.2.
- Do not add new systems until the Founding Stone and builder lifecycle works reliably.

Township v1.0.3
- Debug/lifecycle fix build.
- Added startup/player spawn script-loaded messages so script execution can be verified in-game.
- Removed reliance on block custom component callbacks for founding logic.
- Added global world.afterEvents.playerPlaceBlock handling for Township Founding Stone placement.
- Added global playerBreakBlock cleanup path for Founding Stone removal.
- Added in-memory fallback if dynamic property storage fails.
- Changed @minecraft/server dependency to 1.17.0 to avoid possible module-version loading failure on current non-beta Bedrock.
- Kept BP/RP linking from v1.0.2.


Township v1.0.4
- Stable base: v1.0.3 was confirmed working in-game.
- Added first starter camp construction job after Township Builder arrival.
- Builder now queues a starter camp once spawned.
- Starter camp places simple vanilla blocks one at a time around the Township Founding Stone.
- Starter camp currently uses coarse dirt, campfire, chest, crafting table, torches, oak logs, and oak planks.
- Camp construction is intentionally simple and may overwrite blocks in the small build area for this prototype.
- No roads, lots, storage, economy, or custom builder model added yet.

Current test target for v1.0.4
- Import Township_v1_0_4.mcaddon.
- Confirm BP/RP link together.
- Confirm Township script loaded message.
- Place Township Founding Stone.
- Confirm builder arrives after delay.
- Confirm starter camp builds one block at a time.
- Confirm nearby second Founding Stone is rejected.

--- CONTENT ---
Township v1.0.42

Update workflow:
- Same fixed BP/RP/module UUID identity retained.
- Version bumped to 1.0.42 only.

Purpose of this build:
- v1.0.41 increased the township size, but the initial setup still used four large quadrant jobs. The first quadrant could hang because the loaded setup area and the larger boundary/setup work no longer matched cleanly.

Fixes:
- Replaced the four-quadrant founding setup with sixteen smaller setup sections.
- Each setup section loads separately, works, unloads, then advances to the next section.
- Boundary marking now uses the boundary-radius section when loading, instead of trying to place far-boundary blocks while only the smaller prep-radius section is loaded.
- Added a short wait after each setup ticking area is added so the section has time to load before block work starts.
- Added a small stuck-block failsafe so one failed block placement cannot freeze the entire founding setup forever.
- Villagers no longer spawn during initial setup.

Township v1.0.53

Versioning:
- Same fixed UUID update workflow retained.
- BP/RP manifest versions bumped to 1.0.53.

New Build Lot recorder system:
- Added Township Small Build Lot.
- Added Township Medium Build Lot.
- Added Township Large Build Lot.
- These are special blank lot blocks, not generic recorders.
- Each Build Lot block is placed where the normal lot marker goes.
- When placed inside a township, it registers a blank lot, queues normal lot prep, builds the lot border/fence, and does not auto-build a structure.

Build Lot UI:
- Set Name / Capture Height.
- Save Build.
- Export Saved Build.
- Clear Saved Build.
- Clear Physical Lot.
- Show Lot Info.

Capture settings:
- Capture Down Range controls how far below the lot floor is saved.
- Capture Up Range controls how far above the lot floor is saved.
- The Y settings do not shift the build. They only control the vertical snapshot area.

Export:
- Saved builds export as numbered JSON chunks in chat.
- Export chunks are also sent to the Debug Log Reader hook if installed.
- Export includes build name, lot size, facing, capture ranges, base Y, relative block coordinates, block IDs, and block states when readable.

Clear behavior:
- Clear Saved Build deletes only the stored snapshot.
- Clear Physical Lot clears the build area and restores the blank lot floor while keeping the recorder block and lot border.

Kept:
- Single township radius: 96.
- Command-based ticking areas.
- Existing road/queue changes from v1.0.52.
- Existing building templates.

Township Changelog v1.0.59

Emergency visibility repair after v1.0.57/v1.0.58 testing.

Problem observed:
- In Minecraft, only Township Dirt Road appeared.
- Other Township custom blocks were missing.

Cause identified from package inspection:
- Dirt Road was the only custom block without a custom block component in its block JSON.
- All missing Township blocks had township:* custom component entries.
- On the user's current Bedrock setup, those component entries are causing the blocks to fail or not appear.

Changes in v1.0.59:
- Removed township custom component entries from all Township block JSON files.
- Kept all block identifiers, textures, names, and UUIDs unchanged.
- Restored stable UI access through crouch-near-block checks.
- Added item-use fallback: hold any item and tap/use it on a Township UI block to open its menu if the platform fires itemUseOn.
- Bumped BP/RP manifest versions to 1.0.59.
- Updated script VERSION to 1.0.59.

Expected result:
- Founding Stone, Lot Markers, Build Lots, Build Recorder, Ground Leveler, and Dirt Road should all appear again.
- Direct empty-hand click UI is not used in this build.
- Use crouch near the block or tap it while holding an item for UI access.

Next safe step after this passes:
- Rebuild saved-building features only after the visible block baseline is confirmed working again.

Township v1.0.61 Changelog

Purpose:
Emergency manifest and script dependency repair after v1.0.59/v1.0.60 block visibility failures.

Changes:
- Kept the v1.0.60 custom block visibility approach: no custom component entries in block JSON.
- Kept all Township block JSON files at format_version 1.21.90.
- Corrected @minecraft/server dependency from [1,0,60] to [1,0,47].

- Updated scripts/main.js VERSION constant from 1.0.59 to 1.0.61.
- Bumped BP and RP header/module versions to 1.0.61.
- Preserved all pack UUIDs and module UUIDs.
- Did not add saved-building logic.
- Did not change township generation, radius, road, lot, or ticking-area logic beyond the v1.0.60 state.

Reason:
The v1.0.59 and v1.0.60 manifests incorrectly changed Script API module dependency versions to match the pack version. The prior stable v1.0.56 manifest used @minecraft/server and @minecraft/server-ui version [1,0,47]. Invalid module dependency versions can prevent the Behavior Pack script/module layer from loading correctly.

--- CONTENT ---
Township v1.0.63 Changelog

Purpose:
Emergency rollback/recovery build after v1.0.62 broke the custom blocks again.

Base:
Restored from the confirmed working v1.0.61 recovery checkpoint.

Changes:
- Removed the v1.0.62 direct custom block component entries by returning to the v1.0.61 block JSON state.
- Preserved visible custom Township blocks.
- Bumped BP/RP pack and module versions to 1.0.63.
- Updated main.js internal VERSION constant to 1.0.63.
- Preserved the same Behavior Pack and Resource Pack UUIDs.
- Preserved @minecraft/server and @minecraft/server-ui dependency versions at [1, 0, 47].
- Did not add saved-building logic.
- Did not change township generation, road logic, lot logic, or ticking-area logic.

Research finding:
The v1.0.62 break was caused by re-adding custom block component IDs directly as normal component keys, for example "township:founding_stone_component": {}. In the current official custom component tutorial, block custom components are attached with the "minecraft:custom_components" component list, while the sample manifest uses @minecraft/server version "2.0.0". The direct component-key approach is not safe for this project’s current manifest/API setup.

Test:
- Import v1.0.63.
- Confirm all custom Township blocks appear.
- Do not test direct-click custom components in this build; this is a recovery baseline.
=== SOURCE FILE END ===

Township CHANGELOG v1.0.7

Stable base carried forward:
- v1.0.4 starter camp construction remains the current working camp prototype.
- v1.0.6 lot-prep clearing/leveling remains in place.

v1.0.7 changes:
- Fixed starter camp layout collision where the campfire was placed at the same coordinate as a shelter corner log.
- Moved campfire to a non-corner position inside the starter camp.
- Added Android-friendly status access fallback: crouch/sneak next to the Township Founding Stone to show township status.
- Added item-use fallback: hold any item and tap/use it on the Township Founding Stone to show township status if the platform fires itemUseOn.
- Kept the custom block interaction path and global block interaction path as additional fallbacks.

Known notes:
- Direct empty-hand interaction with the Founding Stone may not fire consistently on Android. For now, use crouch/sneak next to the Founding Stone as the easy status method.
- Builder still wanders like a normal villager. This is tracked for a later builder-control pass.

KIND: TEXT
BYTES: 1510
--- CONTENT ---
Township Changelog v1.0.8

Stable base
- v1.0.7 remains the previous stable checkpoint.
- Kept the working Android crouch-near-Founding-Stone status method.
- Kept the working BP/RP linking, Founding Stone placement, no-overlap rule, builder arrival, and starter camp construction flow.

Changes in v1.0.8
- Added clearer starter camp job phases:
  - clear_lot
  - level_lot
  - build_camp
  - complete
- Status output now includes the current starter camp phase when available.
- Added block-skip logic: if a build location already has the correct block type, the builder skips that placement instead of replacing it again.
- Made the starter camp slightly larger:
  - Expanded the prepared camp area from 5x5 to 7x7.
  - Expanded the shelter frame and roof.
  - Added more torches and adjusted props.
- Kept the Founding Stone protected during clearing/building.
- Added a simple builder-near-town helper. During starter camp construction, if the builder wanders too far from the town center, the script tries to return him near the Founding Stone.
- Reduced camp build interval so the larger camp does not take excessively long to complete.

Known issues / later work
- The Township Builder is still a vanilla villager and may wander when not actively corrected during construction.
- Block-skip logic currently compares block type IDs only. Blocks with important states/facing may need full permutation comparison later.
- The starter camp is still a prototype structure, not the final town center design.

Township CHANGELOG v1.0.9

Stable base: v1.0.7/v1.0.8 lifecycle behavior.

Changes in v1.0.9:
- Improved starter camp layout.
- Replaced the janky internal log/wall layout with a cleaner open pavilion.
- Starter camp now uses a 9x9 prepared area, four corner posts, an open shelter, and a simple roof.
- Added faster skip logic for already-correct blocks.
- Air entries that are already air are now skipped immediately instead of consuming one build delay each.
- Kept Android crouch-near-Founding-Stone status behavior.
- Kept builder nudge-back behavior during construction.

Known issues:
- The Township Builder is still a vanilla villager and can wander outside active construction moments.
- The starter camp is still a prototype structure, not the final central lot/town hall design.
